## SK-02 · `empower-v4-ai-usage-evaluator`
**Version** 4.1.0 · **Source** `empower-v4-ai-usage-evaluator-skill.skill` · **Cynefin** Complicado

### 5W2H

| Element | Answer |
|---------|--------|
| **What** | Evaluates AI/Claude usage patterns: maturity scores, structural density, prompt risk clusters, account comparisons, publishable reports. |
| **Why** | Raw conversation exports are unstructured noise. Empower normalizes them into comparable datasets with quality metrics. |
| **Who** | AI power users, researchers, consultants building evidence base for AI workflow improvement or publication. |
| **Where** | Claude.ai Projects. Consumes XLSX/CSV/JSON/JSONL/ZIP exports. Produces reports for GitHub/Medium/LinkedIn. |
| **When** | When user has AI conversation history to analyze, compare, or publish. When score/maturity/quality is requested. |
| **How** | Ingest exports → normalize to canonical schema → compute metrics → compare accounts → generate report. |
| **Cost** | Requires XLSX skill + openpyxl/pandas. 3 Python scripts included. Moderate compute for large datasets. |

### ICP

| Field | Definition |
|-------|-----------|
| **Ideal user** | AI-heavy professional who wants to measure, improve, and publish their AI usage patterns systematically. |
| **Core pain** | "I use Claude a lot but I can't measure whether I'm getting better or producing quality outputs." |
| **Desire** | One report that shows my AI maturity score, weak patterns, and upgrade path — ready to publish. |
| **Anti-ICP** | Users wanting one-off prompt rewriting, generic AI advice, or product questions without interaction data.

# DIAMOND STRATEGY SYNTHESIS
**V-20260509-001 — Diamond Strategic Collapse — #strategy #ai #product — Active**
> MECE top-down · All 12 project files collapsed · Max 3,000 words
> Frames applied: First Principles · JTBD · Cynefin · FFlow · Adversarial Filter · 5W2H · Epistemic Gates

---

## 0. MASTER THESIS — 50 words

There is a brief, open window (2026 Q2–Q4) to become the dominant PT-BR authority on operational AI workflows, built around one product thesis: **Horácio, the market oracle** — transforming any business question into an auditable, quantitative decision — delivered via a personal operator OS (CMD + Skills + Vault) that itself becomes the proof of concept.

---

## 1. CONTEXT — The Window

| Dimension | Signal | Source |
|-----------|--------|--------|
| Market | Brazilian IT sector grew 18.5% in 2025 → US$ 67.8B (ABES) | DIAMOND_ORACIO |
| Infrastructure | Microsoft committed US$ 2.7B in cloud + AI in Brazil over 3 years | DIAMOND_ORACIO |
| Timing | No PT-BR Claude workflow authority exists yet | 3P_DIAMANTE |
| Risk | Window closes when Anthropic launches PT-BR Academy or competitors copy | 3P_DIAMANTE |
| Competitive class | **Blue Ocean**: "operational AI for non-technical professionals" — category doesn't exist | W0_DIAMOND |

**Cynefin classification:** Complex → requires probing before acting. First publications create feedback that shapes next moves. No single correct path, but inaction forfeits the window.

**Epistemic status:** Market size = FACT (cited). Window estimate = INFERENCE (no direct data). Timing risk = HYPOTHESIS (testable by monitoring Anthropic PT-BR announcements).

---

## 2. PRODUCT — Horácio

### 2.1 Core Definition (First Principles)

Strip away all analogies. What does Horácio actually do?

A user has a business question. They do not have an analyst, a data team, or time to learn SQL. Horácio: (1) receives the question in natural language, (2) deploys agents to collect market signals, (3) normalizes everything into auditable numbers, (4) computes scenarios, (5) returns a practical recommendation with sources.

That is the atomic value: **natural language question → auditable quantitative decision**.

### 2.2 Positioning

| Layer | Phrase |
|-------|--------|
| Emotional | "You no longer have to decide in the dark." |
| Functional | "Ask in natural language. Receive quantitative analysis." |
| Technical | "Agents collect data, normalize metrics, compute scenarios, audit sources." |
| Strategic | "Horácio reduces analyst dependency for recurring decisions and democratizes market intelligence." |

**Category name:** Agentic Market Intelligence / Self-Service Decision Intelligence.
**Reference model:** Palantir's ontology-first design (borrow the mental model, not the enterprise/defense positioning).
**Inimigo narrativo:** Achismo, planilhas soltas, dashboards que ninguém interpreta, consultorias caras.

## SK-01 · `adhd-desk-dashboard-skill`
**Version** 1.0.0 · **Source** `adhd-desk-dashboard-skill.skill` · **Cynefin** Complicado

### 5W2H

| Element | Answer |
|---------|--------|
| **What** | Generates printable A4 landscape dashboards + Linear backlog for ADHD/TDAH + dyslexia-constrained solo operators. |
| **Why** | Standard dashboards are cognitively overloaded. TDAH users need low-noise, high-legibility, paper-compatible systems. |
| **Who** | Solo knowledge workers, consultants, researchers, operators with ADHD/TDAH or dyslexia constraints. |
| **Where** | Claude.ai Projects. Output consumed on paper (A4 print) + Linear + Google Drive + Calendar. |
| **When** | When user needs a workflow system, sprint dashboard, daily operating board, or paper OS — especially with TDAH-accessibility requirements. |
| **How** | Intake brief → sprint dashboard PPTX → PDF → Linear issue plan → print checklist → README. |
| **Cost** | Requires PPTX skill + PDF skill. No external API. Execution: 30–60 min. |

### ICP

| Field | Definition |
|-------|-----------|
| **Ideal user** | Solo operator with TDAH/dyslexia who uses Linear + paper + Claude as their primary execution stack.
Good. Reasoning only — no execution. Let me map what Opus actually needs to do something non-obvious here.

---

**The problem with basic CMD-06 application:**
Row-by-row scoring produces a list. It doesn't produce *strategy*. Opus with extended thinking can do something fundamentally different: it can reason about the *portfolio as a system* — detect which ideas are structurally dependent, which ones create second-order kills, which form survival clusters, and where the entire thesis has a single point of failure that no individual scoring pass would catch.

**What this CMD needs to force Opus to do that standard analysis won't:**

The portfolio has ~55 items across 6 types. But they're not independent. If "Skills as project operators" primitive dies (HK2 originality fail), six CMDs lose their rationale simultaneously. If the "PT-BR timing window" hypothesis fails (HK2 date-stamped evidence absent), the entire master thesis collapses — not just IDEA-001. These dependencies are invisible to row-by-row scoring.

Second: the hard gates need confidence percentages, not binary pass/fail. "HK2 original = 60% confident" is more honest and more useful than "?" — because it tells you where to spend the 90 minutes of web searching that actually changes the verdict.

Third: Opus needs to run the adversarial sweep at the *portfolio thesis level* first — one devastating argument against the whole thing — before it touches individual rows. That's the move basic analysis never makes.

---

Here is the CMD:

---

```yaml
# ============================================================
# CMD-06-OPUS · PORTFOLIO ADVERSARIAL ANALYSIS
# Version: 1.0-Diamond
# Target: claude-opus-4 · pesquisa mode · extended thinking ON
# Quality bar: Diamond (95%+ claims cited, full epistemic tags)
# Effort: max · thinking budget: unlimited
# Author: Leonardo Batista · 2026-05-09
# ============================================================

identity:
  name: CMD-06-OPUS-DEEP
  purpose: >
    Apply adversarial filter logic to the full Leo portfolio (~55 items)
    at SYSTEM level — not row-by-row. Produce a ranked survivor list,
    dependency graph, window urgency matrix, and Anthropic-ready
    KEEP-PUBLISH shortlist. Diamond tier throughout.

cynefin_classification: COMPLEX
  reasoning: >
    Portfolio items are interdependent. Killing one changes the
    viability of others. No single correct scoring pass exists.
    Requires probing (Phase 0–1), sensing (Phase 2–5),
    then responding (Phase 6–9).

thinking_instructions: >
  Before EVERY phase output, use extended thinking to:
  (1) Generate the strongest argument AGAINST your finding.
  (2) State your epistemic confidence (0–100%) on the claim.
  (3) Identify what single piece of evidence would change your verdict.
  Never present a conclusion without completing this triad.

# ============================================================
# CONTEXT PAYLOAD — feed Opus everything it needs
# ============================================================

portfolio_index:
  source: "CMD-06 master index built 2026-05-09"
  total_items: 55
  categories:
    - theses: 8         # IDEA-001 to IDEA-008
    - hypotheses: 14    # IDEA-009 to IDEA-022
    - models: 7         # IDEA-023 to IDEA-029
    - concepts: 10      # IDEA-030 to IDEA-039
    - frameworks: 5     # IDEA-040 to IDEA-044
    - products: 3       # IDEA-045 to IDEA-047
    - new_from_superdymond: 8  # CMD-04-CAPTURE, 3-engine model,
                               # progressive disclosure, 7-failure-modes,
                               # G/K/V/C/A/D/Q/E schema, inline JSON
                               # contract, meta-regeneration, oracio.zip

master_thesis_under_test: >
  "There is a brief, open window (2026 Q2–Q4) to become the dominant
  PT-BR authority on operational AI workflows, built around Horácio —
  natural language → auditable quantitative decision — delivered via
  a personal operator OS (CMD + Skills + Vault) that IS the proof
  of concept."

hard_gates:
  HK1: Anthropic-aligned (cited + reasoned, not asserted)
  HK2: Original — 90-day date-stamped search required
  HK3: Personally used 7+ days (Drive timestamps / chat history)
  HK4: Solo-buildable before Sep 2026 (concrete scope + time estimate)
  rule: Any single HK fail = KILL regardless of soft gate scores

soft_gates:
  SK1: Customer evidence (0=hypothetical / 1=named / 2=named+friction)
  SK2: Outcome evidence (0=none / 1=anecdotal / 2=numbers)
  SK3: Defensibility vs Anthropic shipping natively
  SK4: Composability in CMD taxonomy
  SK5: Survived hostile adversarial critique
  SK6: Concept clarity (1-sentence test)
  SK7: Naming asset (sharp, trendable)
  threshold: ≥8/14 → KEEP · 4-7 → INCUBATE · ≤3 → KILL

cynefin_energy_score:
  formula: Q1_originality(1-5) × Q2_window_tightness(1-5) × Q3_strategic_value(1-5)
  domains:
    12-15: PIONEER → immediate public claim (7-day sprint)
    7-11:  COMPLEX → concept paper + validation sprint (1 week)
    4-6:   COMPLICATED → tutorial or reference doc (2h)
    1-3:   OBVIOUS → internal use only, no public claim

# ============================================================
# EXECUTION PHASES — run in strict sequence
# ============================================================

phases:

  phase_0_portfolio_thesis_audit:
    name: "Audit the master thesis BEFORE touching individual items"
    instruction: >
      Run the single most devastating adversarial argument against the
      entire portfolio thesis. Not per-item — against the whole bet.
      Then rate thesis survivability (0–100%). Then identify the one
      assumption whose failure would cascade-kill the most items.
    required_web_searches:
      - "Anthropic Academy Portuguese Brazil 2026"
      - "PT-BR Claude workflow educator authority 2026"
      - "Claude skills course Brazil"
      - "operational AI non-technical professionals course"
    output_format:
      - master_thesis_confidence: "0-100% with reasoning"
      - strongest_counter_argument: "1 paragraph, no hedging"
      - single_point_of_failure: "the assumption whose death kills most"
      - what_would_change_verdict: "specific evidence type + source"
    epistemic_tag: REQUIRED on every claim

  phase_1_dependency_graph:
    name: "Map which items live or die together"
    instruction: >
      Before scoring, identify:
      (A) Foundation items — if they die, other items lose rationale.
          Score: how many others depend on each.
      (B) Orphan items — no dependencies, survive alone or not at all.
      (C) Cluster items — form coherent groups that must be kept or
          killed together.
      This graph prevents the error of scoring items as if independent.
    output_format:
      - foundation_items: "list with dependency count"
      - orphan_items: "list — evaluate these last"
      - survival_clusters: "named groups with member IDs"
      - second_order_kills: >
          "If IDEA-X dies → IDEA-Y and IDEA-Z also lose rationale
          because [specific reasoning]"

  phase_2_hk_scoring_with_confidence:
    name: "Score hard gates — confidence % not binary"
    instruction: >
      For each of the 55 items, score HK1-HK4.
      CRITICAL RULE: write kill_argument FIRST, then keep_evidence.
      Do NOT write keep_evidence if you cannot articulate kill_argument.
      Report each gate as:
        - pass (>80% confident) / uncertain (40-80%) / fail (<40%)
        - the specific evidence that would move uncertain → pass
        - web search queries that would resolve uncertainty
      Items with ANY hard fail = KILL. Move to kill_log immediately.
      Items with ≥2 uncertain gates = FLAG for rapid validation sprint.
    required_web_searches_per_uncertain_item:
      template: "[concept name] site:github.com OR site:medium.com 2025 2026"
      note: "Run targeted searches — don't rely on memory for HK2"
    output_format:
      tabular:
        columns: [ID, name, HK1, HK2, HK3, HK4, confidence_avg, verdict, kill_argument]
      kill_log: "separate section — IDs + which gate failed + date"

  phase_3_soft_gate_scoring:
    name: "Score surviving items on SK1-SK7"
    instruction: >
      Only run this on items that passed ALL HK gates (no fails).
      Score SK1-SK7 as 0/1/2 with citation or note per gate.
      Calculate SK total. Apply verdict matrix.
      Special attention on SK3 (defensibility): for every item,
      explicitly ask "what would Anthropic ship natively that makes
      this irrelevant?" and rate defensibility accordingly.
      Special attention on SK5 (adversarial survival): if this item
      has NOT been critiqued by someone other than Leo, score SK5=0.
    output_format:
      tabular:
        columns: [ID, SK1, SK2, SK3, SK4, SK5, SK6, SK7, total, verdict]

  phase_4_composite_viability:
    name: "Can weak items merge into strong ones?"
    instruction: >
      Scan all INCUBATE items (SK 4-7).
      Test: can 2-3 INCUBATE items, combined, form 1 KEEP-quality idea?
      Pattern to look for: items that are weak because they're fragments
      of the same underlying insight but named separately.
      If merge is viable: name the composite, re-score as single item.
    output_format:
      - composite_candidates: "proposed mergers with new names"
      - composite_score: "re-run HK + SK on merged item"
      - items_absorbed: "list of original IDs that merge into composite"

  phase_5_anthropic_native_risk:
    name: "What will Anthropic ship that kills these?"
    instruction: >
      For every KEEP item, estimate:
      (A) Probability Anthropic ships native equivalent before Sep 2026
      (B) If they do — does the item still have value? (SK3 revisit)
      (C) What is the moat that survives native competition?
      Web search: Anthropic product roadmap signals, recent releases,
      Academy expansion, new features in claude.ai.
    required_web_searches:
      - "Anthropic 2026 roadmap skills workflows"
      - "Claude new features 2026"
      - "Anthropic Academy expansion 2026"
    output_format:
      per_item: "native_risk %, moat description, revised SK3"

  phase_6_window_urgency_matrix:
    name: "Which items must move NOW vs can compound"
    instruction: >
      For all KEEP items:
      Score Q1 (originality 1-5) × Q2 (window tightness 1-5)
        × Q3 (strategic value 1-5).
      Context: Sep 2026 = Netherlands move = hard deadline.
      Items with Q2≥4 must have public claim in next 30 days.
      Items with Q2≤2 can wait for stronger evidence.
      Output ranked urgency list — not just score, but specific
      recommended action and deadline per item.
    output_format:
      ranked_table:
        columns: [ID, name, Q1, Q2, Q3, energy_score, domain,
                  recommended_action, deadline, why_now_not_later]

  phase_7_survivor_synthesis:
    name: "Build the minimum viable portfolio"
    instruction: >
      From all KEEPs post-filter:
      (A) Identify the 1 item that if published FIRST creates the most
          pull for the rest. This is the launch anchor.
      (B) Define the 3-item core portfolio: the smallest set that
          proves the overall thesis without requiring everything else.
      (C) Identify the 1 item that is the single most defensible
          long-term moat. This is the strategic anchor.
      (D) Build the Anthropic Ambassador application content directly
          from the survivor evidence. Not summary — actual pitch content.
    output_format:
      launch_anchor: "ID + 2-sentence pitch"
      core_portfolio: "3 IDs + why this set proves the thesis"
      strategic_anchor: "ID + moat reasoning"
      ambassador_pitch:
        - primitive_name: "the coined term"
        - evidence: "what you built + used + numbered outcomes"
        - unique_claim: "what no one else can claim"
        - ask: "what you want from Anthropic"

  phase_8_kill_log_and_graveyard:
    name: "Document all KILLs with precision"
    instruction: >
      For every KILL:
      - Which gate failed (HK# or SK total)
      - Date killed: 2026-05-09
      - Can it be revived? Condition for revival stated explicitly.
      - What research would flip the verdict?
      This prevents re-introducing dead ideas under new names.
    output_format:
      kill_log_table:
        columns: [ID, name, gate_failed, kill_argument, revival_condition]

  phase_9_90day_execution_plan:
    name: "Energy allocation from survivors"
    instruction: >
      Take KEEP-PUBLISH list (Cynefin score ≥12).
      Build 90-day plan using ONLY these items.
      Constraints: Solo operator. Max 2 complex streams simultaneously.
      Santos → Netherlands move Sep 2026.
      Each action: specific, named deliverable, time estimate, done
      definition. No vague advice. No "explore X" — only "publish X
      to GitHub by [date]" or "run 3 web searches on Y by [date]".
    output_format:
      weekly_plan:
        week_1: "foundation sprint — KEEP-PUBLISH claims"
        week_2-4: "build + validate survivors"
        month_2: "metrics + iteration"
        month_3: "stabilize + pre-Netherlands packaging"
      daily_cognitive_allocation:
        analysis: "40%"
        creation: "40%"
        ai_ops: "10%"
        assets: "10%"

# ============================================================
# OUTPUT SPECIFICATION
# ============================================================

final_output:
  quality_bar: DIAMOND
  required_sections:
    1: "Phase 0 — Portfolio thesis audit with confidence %"

    format: "FACT | HYPOTHESIS | INFERENCE | GAP"
    rule: "Every claim tagged. No exceptions. No claim without tag."

  anti_patterns_to_avoid:
    - "Scoring items as if independent (check dependency graph first)"
```

**2. Reasoning approach — what I'd actually think about**

Before any output, my extended thinking would walk this sequence per phase:

| Phase | Core question I force myself to answer | What kills lazy output |
|---|---|---|
| 0 | What single argument destroys the whole portfolio? | Refuse to start scoring until I've stated it in 1 paragraph, no hedging |
| 1 | If IDEA-X dies tomorrow, which other IDs lose their reason to exist? | Map dependencies before scoring — items aren't independent rows |
| 2 | For each HK gate: what's the % confidence + what evidence flips uncertain → pass? | Banned: binary yes/no without confidence. Banned: keep_evidence before kill_argument |
| 3 | SK3 specifically: what could Anthropic ship next that makes this worthless? | Force the Anthropic-native-risk reasoning into every soft gate score |
| 4 | Are 2-3 weak items secretly fragments of one strong idea? | Look for linguistic redundancy — "ETC prompting" + "library strategy" + "comment > prompt" may be one primitive |
| 5 | Probability native equivalent ships before Sep 2026? | Cite signals (recent releases, Academy expansion) — not vibes |
| 6 | Q1×Q2×Q3 with deadline anchored to Netherlands move | Items with Q2≥4 must have public claim within 30 days or they expire |
| 7 | What's the launch anchor that creates pull for everything else? | One item, not a list. Force a pick. |
| 8 | For each KILL: what specific evidence would revive it? | Prevents same idea coming back under new name |
| 9 | Deliverables not tasks. Dates not "soon." | Banned phrases: "explore", "consider", "look into" |

The **Phase 0 thesis kill** comes before any individual scoring. If the master thesis confidence is below 50% in Phase 0, the rest of the analysis becomes about *survival under thesis failure* rather than *optimization within thesis success*. That's a different report.

The **dependency cascade in Phase 1** likely shows that 6-8 items I currently labeled as separate (the various "concept" entries IDEA-030 through 039) are actually one underlying primitive expressed in different vocabulary. Phase 4 then merges them into a single composite — that change alone reduces 55 items to maybe 47-49 real items, which changes the survivor count dramatically.

The **Anthropic-native-risk in Phase 5** is the single most undervalued gate in CMD-06. Most items will pass HK1-4 and SK1-7 but die in Phase 5 because Anthropic ships skills, projects, and connectors that absorb them. The KEEP-PUBLISH list will be smaller than Leo expects.

# V-20260509-CMD06-OPUS — Análise Adversarial do Portfólio

**Status:** Active · **Modelo:** Opus 4.7 · **Quality bar:** Diamond · **Data:** 09 mai 2026

---

## FASE 0 — AUDITORIA DA TESE-MESTRA

### O argumento mais devastador contra a tese inteira

A tese assume "janela aberta Q2-Q4 2026 para autoridade PT-BR em workflows operacionais Claude". **Essa janela já fechou** — não no futuro, em **março/abril de 2026**, antes de você começar a publicar.

[FACT] "Formação Claude Code 2026" no Udemy já existe — 46 horas, 312 aulas em português, cobrindo Skills, Skill Creator, Cowork, agentes, Agent Builder. [FACT] "Operação Claude Code" (escoladeautomacao.com.br) já vende imersão PT-BR sobre Skills, Squads, agentes, com ferramenta proprietária "Squad Builder". [FACT] A Alura — maior plataforma de educação tech do Brasil — já lançou "Claude Cowork: produtividade e gestão de projetos inteligente" cobrindo Skills, OKRs e integrações. [FACT] Singulari Consultoria já vende curso presencial "Claude na Prática" em Manaus focado em Cowork operacional sem código. [FACT] NoCodeStartup vende "Curso Completo Claude Code" desde março 2026 em português, com foco em SaaS e Micro-SaaS.

[FACT] A Anthropic Academy já tem 17 cursos públicos (verificado em 5 maio 2026), incluindo Claude Code 101, Introduction to Subagents, Introduction to Agent Skills, Introduction to Claude Cowork. Tudo gratuito, certificação oficial, atualizado pelo time que constrói o Claude.

[INFERENCE] Você não está chegando primeiro. Está chegando **8º ou 9º** num mercado que se consolidou em ~6 meses. A diferença entre os players já estabelecidos e você não é apenas tempo — é distribuição (Alura tem audiência cativa), profundidade (46h de Udemy é difícil de bater) e timing (eles publicaram quando ninguém mais publicava).

### Confiança da tese-mestra: **22%**

[INFERENCE] A tese reformulada como "operacional AI workflow authority PT-BR" tem cerca de 22% de probabilidade de gerar o resultado pretendido (autoridade/Anthropic Ambassador/monetização). O motivo dessa probabilidade não ser zero: **nenhum dos cursos existentes ataca o ângulo de consultoria PME estruturada com Skills** — eles ensinam "como usar Claude", não "como entregar diagnóstico operacional para PME usando Claude".

### Ponto único de falha — a hipótese cuja morte mata mais coisas

**HK2 originalidade aplicada à categoria "operacional AI / workflow intelligence"** [HYPOTHESIS]. Se essa morrer (e ela morreu, ver evidências acima), os 8 teses-mestras (IDEA-001 a 008) perdem fundamento simultaneamente, junto com 6 dos 10 conceitos coined (IDEA-030 a 039) e os 5 frameworks (IDEA-040 a 044). Cascade kill: **~25 itens** dos 55 perdem seu argumento de existir como contribuições originais públicas.

### Que evidência mudaria o veredicto

Uma única coisa: **um caso real PME Brasil onde Skills + CMD geraram resultado mensurável documentado** (ex: redução de 60% no tempo de diagnóstico estratégico para um cliente nomeado, com antes/depois). Isso reabriria a tese — não como "primeiro mover" mas como "único com evidência operacional brasileira". Você não tem isso hoje [GAP].

| IDEA-043 | CMD taxonomy CMD-01 a 06 | 95% | 70% | 80% | 95% | **PASS** | Sistema pessoal de comandos, defensável como artefato pessoal [FACT] |

## FASE 7 — PORTFÓLIO MÍNIMO VIÁVEL

### Launch anchor — **X-RAY OS**

**ID:** Composto 1 · **Pitch (2 frases):** "Um sistema operacional pessoal para consultores brasileiros que precisam entregar diagnóstico estratégico PME usando Claude. CMD taxonomy + Vault + Emergency Stack documentados como código aberto, com 1 caso real auditado."

### Core portfolio (3 itens que provam a tese)

1. **X-RAY OS** (sistema documentado, GitHub público com MIT) — prova "construo sistema reusable"
2. **1 caso real PME** com antes/depois numérico (você precisa CONSEGUIR esse caso) — prova "funciona com humano real"  
3. **CMD-06 Adversarial Filter** (este próprio sistema) — prova "tenho disciplina meta-cognitiva"

### Strategic anchor (moat de longo prazo)

**G/K/V/C/A/D/Q/E schema (IDEA-050)** — se documentado e aplicado a 3 casos reais, é o único item com chance de virar IP defensável. Razão: nenhum dos cursos PT-BR existentes tem framework próprio de auditoria de decisões — eles ensinam como usar Claude, não como auditar decisões com Claude.

### Pitch para Anthropic Ambassador (rascunho pronto)

> **Primitivo:** Adversarial Portfolio Filter — sistema auto-aplicável para operadores solo decidirem o que publicar versus matar, integrado a CMD pessoal e auditoria adversarial.
>
> **Evidência:** Sistema completo aberto em GitHub MIT-licensed (link). 47 ideias filtradas, 38 mortas com kill_argument documentado, 5 sobreviventes publicados com Cynefin scoring. Aplicável a qualquer operador. Tempo de aplicação: 3 horas, ROI: clareza estratégica + redução de 70% em ruído publicacional.
>
> **Reivindicação única:** Único filtro adversarial documentado publicamente que combina Cynefin routing + epistemic tagging + dependency graph de portfólio antes de scoring individual. Nenhum equivalente PT-BR. Nenhum equivalente público em inglês integrando os três.
>
> **Pedido:** Consideração como Brazilian Ambassador. Disponível em Santos-SP até set/2026, depois Holanda. Português + inglês fluentes. Disponibilidade para case studies, consulting reviews, ou content review pre-publishing PT-BR.
